Impress your friends around with a truly unique and exclusive watch face at your wrist.<br>  <br><b>UNIQUE FEATURES</b><br>Works for square, round and triangle screens<br>Best displaying at night and in daylight<br>Superb readability<br>Modern, old-school, avant-garde, retro, futuristic and fashion, all at same time<br>Require zero user interaction<br>Original design by professional artist, this is not a copy of any real brand<br>Animations from dimmed state to visible state<br>Fully functional<br>A clean minimal watch face with an accent of color<br>Color customization (available in 0 color)<br>Works even with 0% battery<br>Will take care of your battery like no other watch face does<br>Dimmed state for extended battery life<br>Beautifully express the giant void in the universe<br>Analog or digital, you choose!<br>Premium look with Ultra HD<br>A custom engine forged by hand<br>Will bypass the recent bug concerning round detection<br>For men and women<br>Support every languages<br>Dark theme<br>Android Wear design guidelines compliant<br>Will save you from your precious time<br>A relative lack of superlatives since almost everyone is using them<br>Luxuriously, luxurious or luxury, because many other watch faces use these words<br>No ads<br>Material design compatible<br>Did we use awesome?<br>Get nothing for free instead of paying for nothing<br>Lightest watch face ever (37714 bytes only)<br>May differ from screenshots, watch not included<br>  <br>Having a clean background for polished video in your Google Play listing.<br>Should definitely save a bit more of your battery compared to any watch face (animated or not).<br>We already have the time almost everywhere and many of us are used to not wear a watch that gives time since our teenage-hood.<br>  <br>You can use this Watch Face on any Android Wear wearables, including non exhaustively:<br> ASUS ZenWatch<br> LG Watch R<br> LG G Watch<br> Moto 360<br> Samsung Gear Live<br> Sony SmartWatch 3 SWR50<br> Wear Emulator<br>  <br>As not seen on TV.<br>  <br>&quot;Perfection is achieved, not when there is nothing more to add, but when there is nothing left to take away.&quot;  Antoine de Saint-Exupry, <i>Airman&#39;s Odyssey</i><br>  <br>  <br>Wait 10 to 20 seconds after installing this watch face in order to be able to select it.<br>If it is still not available, open the Android Wear app on your handheld and select &quot;Resync apps&quot; in the settings.<br>  <br>  <br>\_()_/</div>  <div class="show-more-end"></div> </div> <div> <button class="play-button show-more coupled with real-time filters, effects, randomness and a live approach.<p><br>THIS IS THE FREE VERSION<br>Ads are displayed and you cannot save or load any presets.<br>Remove the ads and unlock all Linear and logarithmic knobs and bars<br> - Visual pitches synced with the tempo<br> - 1x TR-808 drum machine style and sounds<br> - 1x TR-909 drum machine <br> - 2x TB-303 bassline / groovebox<br> - 1x Metropolis-like sequencer (MPL-185)<br> - Independent (but synced) sequencer clock for each machine<br> - Steps divider and reverser<br> - Resolution from 1/128 to 1/2<br> - Independent mixer levels for the drum machine, the bass lines and fxs<br> - Independent levels, mutes and solos for each drum instrument<br> - Memory of 4 banks of 8 patterns with 16 instruments containing 16 steps maximum each<br> - Memory of 4 banks of 8 patterns with 39 notes containing 16 steps maximum each<br> - Bank and step sequencing loop (disabled, sequential, reverse, ping-pong, random or brownian)<br> - Real-time chained effects (Compressor, Flanger, Phaser, Distortion, Delay, Moog filters, Formant and Bitcrusher) with various parameters<br> - Audio FFT visualizer (waveform and frequency bands)<br> Tales of Pocoro is a unique and interesting puzzle game with gorgeous and cute RPG graphics for *Android Wear* wearables.<br>  <br>Enjoy more than 200 levels and 3 levels of difficulty.<br>Unlock new characters and random mode for unlimited fun at your wrist!<br>  <br>You can play &quot;Tales of Pocoro&quot; on any Android Wear devices, including:<br> ASUS ZenWatch<br> LG Watch R<br> LG G Watch<br> Moto 360<br> Samsung Gear Live<br> Sony SmartWatch 3 SWR50<br>  <br>GAMES RULES<br>Tales of Pocoro is a puzzle game where the goal is to reach the exit. However to make things a bit more interesting, you will have to clear other strange columns before exiting to achieve the level.<br>There are 3 levels of difficulty, the harder you choose the more columns you will have.<br>    <br>HOW TO PLAY<br> Move your character by swiping or tapping the arrows (keyboard and trackball are also supported).<br> Long press the screen to pause the game and spawn the menu options.<br> Put your palm completely over the screen until it vibrates to quickly exit and dim the screen.<br> Double-tap (very fast) anywhere on the screen to control the camera via swiping.<br> Double-tap (very fast) again to stop moving the camera.<br>    <br>This game is a pure indie game, made on the spare time of Curved Cat Games and ported by AQ on Android Wear. We hope you will enjoy playing it as much as we did while coding it. <br>  <br>We will never claim to be the best wearable game, nor the most addictive game for Android Wear. Instead, we focus on providing a compatible experience with wearable devices without breaking the paradigm of the Android Wear platform, and with love. class="display-price">$1.99</span>   </button>    </span>      </span> </div> <div class="description">  Tired of games like snake, 2048 copies, Flappy clones and tic-tac-toe on your smartwatch? &quot;Castle Wear&quot; is an old-school persistent turn-based rogue-like game influenced by heroic fantasy, currently in alpha stage development for your wearable devices.<br>  <br>You can play &quot;Castle Wear&quot; on any of the following device.<br> Android Wear (ASUS ZenWatch, LG G Watch, LG Watch R, Moto 360, Samsung Gear Live, Sony SmartWatch 3 SWR50)<br> Sony SmartWatch (SW2, NM2)<br> Any Android device running 2.3 (API 9) or greater<br>  <br>IMPORTANT NOTE<br>Please be indulgent concerning the bugs, crashes, lack of content and the high difficulty, &quot;Castle Wear&quot; is in ALPHA stage development, a very early state part of the alpha funding program. We do not work on it in full time, but expect at least weekly update, the game is simply under construction.<br>Keep also in mind the game is originally targeting little screens, the Android device version is simply a convenient bonus. There are many bugs which we are aware of (or not), lot of features not yet implemented, many performance bottlenecks, a lot of content is missing and there is no manual yet. Carry on.<p>You can support us in many ways, from small favors as talking and sharing about this game to bigger ones, like buying &quot;Castle Wear&quot; or sending us constructive feedback.<p>By supporting us in buying &quot;Castle Wear&quot;, you make an investment in this game and its further development.<br>You will receive all future updates without any cost involved, and you will be freed from any potential price increase. And in the contrary of crowdfunding, you already have a &quot;playable&quot; (but unfinished) game in your hands.<br>  <br>PLOT<br>The evil sorcerer Diordna stole a very rare talisman from the King and generated a mysterious maze with its power under the King&#39;s Castle. Since then the King has gone mad and has started to continuously send new recruits further down in the maze to retrieve the previous artifact from the hands of Diordna.<br>  <br>NAVIGATION<br> Swipe up and swipe down to move through menu options.<br> Swipe to the left to go back or cancel the current screen.<br> Swipe to the right to select the current menu option.<br>  <br>TIPS FOR STARTING<br> Weigh your party (e.g. take two fighters, a thief, a cleric and two mages).<br> Do not run in the wall, it makes noise and that might alert nearby monsters.<br> Remember where your last party died, you can retrieve their corpses with another party later on.<br> Be cautious with spells points. You can only refill them via resting in the Adventurer&#39;s Inn.<br> You can only level up in the Adventurer&#39;s Inn.<br> The difficulty is high, so do not worry if you die many times.<br>  <br>FEATURES ALREADY THERE<br> Custom character creation, 8 classes (e.g. Cleric), 5 different races (e.g. Elf), gold, exp and many attributes<br> 50 unique spells split into Mage and Cleric categories, divided into 7 levels of power and varying effects<br> Hundred of items and hundred of monsters<br> Few NPC available (e.g. Trading center, Temple)<br> An underground textured 3D maze (raycasting) with several levels infested of monsters<br> A turn-by-turn combat system allowing various actions per member<br> Non persistent auto-map<br>  <br>FUTURE FEATURES<br>They more or less depend on time and your support, the list is non exhaustive.<br> Better UI, better performance<br> Cloud save, quest system, achievements and rewards<br> Real-time multi-player battle mode (fight with your friends)<br> Procedural random level generation<br> A real story-line<br> Multi-class mode (fighter-mage, paladin, rogue and archbishop)<br> Bestiary, weaponry, Mini manual<br>  <br>  <br> Thank <div class="details"> <a class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=org.quet.android.visualizer" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <h2> <a class="title" href="/store/apps/details?id=org.quet.android.visualizer" title="Visualizer for SmartWatch">    Visualizer for SmartWatch  <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> </h2>  <div class="subtitle-container">  <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=AQ" title="AQ">AQ</a>   <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span>   <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="org.quet.android.visualizer"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">1</div> <button class="price buy">    <span class="display-price">$1.99</span>   </button>    </span>      </span> </div> <div class="description">  Party like it&#39;s 2999 with a colorful glowing display on your SmartWatch that dynamically changes with any ambient sound or music, in real-time.<p>Visualizer is an Android extension for SmartWatch which will visualize your microphone input or what your device is playing, depending on the mode you selected.<p>Actions<br>PRESS the screen on the right or on the left to switch from a visualizer preset to another.<br>PRESS the screen on the top or on the bottom to increase or decrease the blur effect.<br>SWIPE the screen to the left or to the right to add more or less rotation effect.<br>LONG PRESS the screen to select the mode you want: recording mode or playing mode.<p>Visualizer renderers (preset)<br>- Linear waveform<br>- Circular waveform<br>- Vertical bars (passive equalizer)<br>- Circular bars<br>- Tree fractal<br>- Mandelbrot fractal (experimental)<p>System requirements<br>- Android 2.3 or greater<br>- Sony SmartWatch 1 or 2<br>- Smart Connect (LiveWare Mgr)<p>About requested permissions<br>android.permission.MODIFY_AUDIO_SETTINGS<br>CHANGE YOUR AUDIO SETTINGS is only used for the real-time audio waveform visualizer in &quot;playing mode&quot;.<p>android.permission.RECORD_AUDIO<br>RECORD AUDIO is only used for the real-time audio waveform visualizer in &quot;recording mode&quot;, nothing is recorded. Stated from http://developer.android.com/reference/android/media/audiofx/Visualizer.html: [...]to protect privacy of certain audio data (e.g voice mail) the use of the visualizer requires the permission android.permission.RECORD_AUDIO<p>Note: This application will not be visible in your phones home screen. href="/store/apps/details?id=org.quet.android.conway" title="Conway's game for SmartWatch">    Conway's game for SmartWatch  <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> </h2>  <div class="subtitle-container">  <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=AQ" title="AQ">AQ</a>   <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span>   <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="org.quet.android.conway"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">1</div> <button class="price buy">    <span class="display-price">$1.99</span>   </button>    </span>      </span> </div> <div class="description">  Conway&#39;s Game of Life for SmartWatch.<p>The Game of Life, is not really a game but a cellular automaton (John Horton Conway, 1970) which can live, reproduce or die. Observe how cells evolves on your SmartWatch screen.<p>ACTIONS<br>- Touch will toggle HUD visibility (displaying FPS &amp; stats)<br>- Long touch will wipe all the cells from the screen (generation reset)<br>- Swipe will send a &quot;glider&quot; heading towards swipe direction<br>- Shake strongly the watch to randomize life<p>FEATURES<br>- Generation speed / FPS<br>- Custom world size (from 8x8 to 64x64)<br>- Managed screen state (&quot;off&quot;, &quot;dim&quot;, &quot;on&quot; or &quot;auto&quot;)<br>- Cosmectic changes (grid color, cell color, cell shape, anti-aliasing)<p>INTRINSIC GAME RULES<br>1. Any live cell with fewer than two live neighbours dies, as if caused by under-population.<br>2. Any live cell with two or three live neighbours lives on to the next generation.<br>3. Any live cell with more than three live neighbours dies, as if by overcrowding.<br>4. Any dead cell with exactly three live neighbours becomes a live cell, as if by reproduction.<p>More information on Wikipedia: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conway&#39;s_Game_of_Life<p>Note: This application will not be visible in your phones home screen. Access Applications via Smart Connect.<p><br>Smart Connect extension for SmartWatch 2<p><br>LiveWare extension for SmartWatch</p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a
